Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing the Colossus 237 program listing from the private collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin, and then modifying pre-existing Colossus 249 (Apollo 9) source files to incorporate changes. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 237 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS 
	BY NASA 2021111-031  1:17 AUG. 24, 1968


012871,000002:                                                                                                 #  Copyright:    Public domain.
012872,000003:                                                                                                 #  Filename:      PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
012873,000004:                                                                                                 #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Colossus build 237.
012874,000005:                                                                                                 #                This is for the Command Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance
012875,000006:                                                                                                 #                Computer (AGC), we believe for Apollo 8.
012876,000007:                                                                                                 #  Assembler:    yaYUL
012877,000008:                                                                                                 #  Contact:      Jim Lawton <jim DOT lawton AT gmail DOT com>
012878,000009:                                                                                                 #  Website:      www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
012879,000010:                                                                                                 #  Page scans:   www.ibiblio.org/apollo/ScansForConversion/Colossus237/
012880,000011:                                                                                                 #  Mod history:  2011-01-23 JL   Adapted from corresponding Colossus 249 file.
012881,000012: 
012882,000013:                                                                                                 # # Page 300
012883,000014: 
012884,000015:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012885,000016:                                                                                                 #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
012886,000017:                                                                                                 #  MOD BY - FILENE
012887,000018:                                                                                                 #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012888,000019: 
012889,000020:                                                                                                 #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
012890,000021: 
012891,000022:                                                                                                 #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012892,000023:                                                                                                 #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012893,000024:                                                                                                 #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012894,000025:                                                                                                 #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAM, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012895,000026:                                                                                                 #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012896,000027:                                                                                                 #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012897,000028:                                                                                                 #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012898,000029:                                                                                                 #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012899,000030:                                                                                                 #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012900,000031: 
012901,000032:                                                                                                 #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012902,000033:                                                                                                 #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
012903,000034:                                                                                                 #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012904,000035:                                                                                                 #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
012905,000036:                                                                                                 #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
012906,000037:                                                                                                 #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
012907,000038: 
012908,000039: 
012909,000040:                                                                                                 #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
012910,000041: 
012911,000042:                                                                                                 #  KEYBOARD:
012912,000043:                                                                                                 #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012913,000044:                                                                                                 #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012914,000045:                                                                                                 #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012915,000046:                                                                                                 #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012916,000047:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012917,000048: 
012918,000049:                                                                                                 #  UPLINK:
012919,000050:                                                                                                 #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
012920,000051:                                                                                                 #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012921,000052:                                                                                                 #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012922,000053: 
012923,000054:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012924,000055:                                                                                                 #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012925,000056:                                                                                                 #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012926,000057:                                                                                                 #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
012927,000058:                                                                                                 #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012928,000059: 
012929,000060: 
012930,000061:                                                                                                 #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
012931,000062: 
012932,000063:                                                                                                 #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
012933,000064:                                                                                                 #            1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
012934,000065:                                                                                                 # # Page 301
012935,000066:                                                                                                 #            2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
012936,000067:                                                                                                 #               PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
012937,000068:                                                                                                 #               RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTEDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
012938,000069:                                                                                                 #               CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
012939,000070:                                                                                                 #               ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
012940,000071:                                                                                                 #            3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
012941,000072:                                                                                                 #               SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
012942,000073:                                                                                                 #               30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
012943,000074:                                                                                                 #            4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
012944,000075:                                                                                                 #               ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
012945,000076:                                                                                                 #               THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT 40.
012946,000077: 
012947,000078:                                                                                                 #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
012948,000079:                                                                                                 #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
012949,000080:                                                                                                 #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012950,000081: 
012951,000082: 
012952,000083:                                                                                                 #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
012953,000084: 
012954,000085:                                                                                                 #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
012955,000086:                                                                                                 #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
012956,000087:                                                                                                 #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
012957,000088: 
012958,000089:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
012959,000090:                                                                                                 #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
012960,000091:                                                                                                 #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
012961,000092:                                                                                                 #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
012962,000093:                                                                                                 #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
012963,000094:                                                                                                 #            1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
012964,000095:                                                                                                 #            2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
012965,000096: 
012966,000097:                                                                                                 #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
012967,000098:                                                                                                 #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
012968,000099: 
012969,000100: 
012970,000101:                                                                                                 #  OUTPUT-
012971,000102: 
012972,000103:                                                                                                 #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
012973,000104:                                                                                                 #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
012974,000105:                                                                                                 #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
012975,000106:                                                                                                 #  IN INTERRUPT.
012976,000107: 
012977,000108: 
012978,000109:                                                                                                 #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
012979,000110: 
012980,000111:                                                                                                 #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
012981,000112:                                                                                                 #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
012982,000113:                                                                                                 #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
012983,000114:                                                                                                 #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
012984,000115: 
012985,000116:                                                                                                 # # Page 302
012986,000117: 
012987,000118:                                                                                                 #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
012988,000119:                                                                                                 #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
012989,000120: 
012990,000121: 
012991,000122:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
012992,000123: 
012993,000124:                                                                                                 #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
012994,000125:                                                                                                 #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
012995,000126: 
012996,000127:                                                                                                 #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
012997,000128:                                                                                                 #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
012998,000129:                                                                                                 #                                      NVSUBUSY
012999,000130:                                                                                                 #                                      PRENVBSY
013000,000131: 
013001,000132:                                                                                                 #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO TO SLEEP WHILE
013002,000133:                                                                                                 #                AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013003,000134: 
013004,000135:                                                                                                 #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013005,000136:                                                                                                 #              PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013006,000137:                                                                                                 #              (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013007,000138:                                                                                                 #              FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013008,000139: 
013009,000140:                                                                                                 #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013010,000141:                                                                                                 #                 COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013011,000142: 
013012,000143:                                                                                                 #     JAMTERM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013013,000144:                                                                                                 #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
013014,000145: 
013015,000146:                                                                                                 #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013016,000147: 
013017,000148:                                                                                                 #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013018,000149:                                                                                                 #                   REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013019,000150:                                                                                                 #                   THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013020,000151:                                                                                                 #                   SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013021,000152: 
013022,000153:                                                                                                 #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013023,000154:                                                                                                 #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013024,000155: 
013025,000156:                                                                                                 #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013026,000157:                                                                                                 #     TABLES:.
013027,000158: 
013028,000159: 
013029,000160:                                                                                                 #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013030,000161:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013031,000162:                                                                                                 #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013032,000163: 
013033,000164: 
013034,000165:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
013035,000166: 
013036,000167:                                                                                                 #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
013037,000168:                                                                                                 # # Page 303
013038,000169:                                                                                                 #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
013039,000170:                                                                                                 #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
013040,000171: 
013041,000172:                                                                                                 #                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
013042,000173: 
013043,000174: 
013044,000175:                                                                                                 #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
013045,000176: 
013046,000177: 
013047,000178:                                                                                                 #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013048,000179: 
013049,000180:                                                                                                 #  DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   # DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013050,000181:                                                                                                 #  DECBRNCH       ERASE                   # +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013051,000182:                                                                                                 #  VERBREG        ERASE                   # VERB CODE
013052,000183:                                                                                                 #  NOUNREG        ERASE                   # NOUN CODE
013053,000184:                                                                                                 #  XREG           ERASE                   # R1 INPUT BUFFER
013054,000185:                                                                                                 #  YREG           ERASE                   # R2 INPUT BUFFER
013055,000186:                                                                                                 #  ZREG           ERASE                   # R3 INPUT BUFFER
013056,000187:                                                                                                 #  XREGLP ERASE                   # LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013057,000188:                                                                                                 #  YREGLP ERASE                   # LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013058,000189:                                                                                                 #  HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013059,000190:                                                                                                 #                                         #          MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013060,000191:                                                                                                 #  ZREGLP ERASE                   # LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013061,000192:                                                                                                 #  LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          # TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013062,000193:                                                                                                 #                                         #          MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013063,000194:                                                                                                 #  MODREG ERASE                   # MODE CODE
013064,000195:                                                                                                 #  DSPLOCK        ERASE                   # KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013065,000196:                                                                                                 #  REQRET ERASE                   # RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013066,000197:                                                                                                 #  LOADSTAT       ERASE                   # STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013067,000198:                                                                                                 #  CLPASS ERASE                   # PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013068,000199:                                                                                                 #  NOUT           ERASE                   # ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013069,000200:                                                                                                 #  NOUNCADR       ERASE                   # MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013070,000201:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE        ERASE                   # N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013071,000202:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE1       ERASE                   # NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS1) =MONSAVE +1
013072,000203:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE2       ERASE                   # NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013073,000204:                                                                                                 #  DSPTAB ERASE           +13D    # 0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
013074,000205:                                                                                                 #  CADRSTOR       ERASE                   # ENDIDLE STORAGE
013075,000206:                                                                                                 #  NVQTEM ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013076,000207:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013077,000208:                                                                                                 #  NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   # NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013078,000209:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = NVQTEM+1
013079,000210:                                                                                                 #  VERBSAVE       ERASE                   # NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013080,000211:                                                                                                 #  DSPLIST        ERASE                   # WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013081,000212:                                                                                                 #  EXTVBACT       ERASE                   # EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013082,000213:                                                                                                 #  DSPTEM1        ERASE           +2      # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013083,000214:                                                                                                 #  DSPTEM2        ERASE           +2      # BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013084,000215:                                                                                                 #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013085,000216: 
013086,000217: 
013087,000218:                                                                                                 #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013088,000219: 
013089,000220:                                                                                                 # # Page 304
013090,000221:                                                                                                 #  DSEXIT =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR DSPIN
013091,000222:                                                                                                 #  EXITEM =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
013092,000223:                                                                                                 #  BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         # RETURN FOR 2BLANK
013093,000224: 
013094,000225:                                                                                                 #  WRDRET =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR 5BLANK
013095,000226:                                                                                                 #  WDRET          =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR DSPWD
013096,000227:                                                                                                 #  DECRET =       INTBIT15        # RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
013097,000228:                                                                                                 #  21/22REG       =       INTBIT15        # TEMP FOR CHARIN
013098,000229: 
013099,000230:                                                                                                 #  UPDATRET       =       POLISH          # RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
013100,000231:                                                                                                 #  CHAR           =       POLISH          # TEMP FOR CHARIN
013101,000232:                                                                                                 #  ERCNT          =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
013102,000233:                                                                                                 #  DECOUNT        =       POLISH          # COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
013103,000234: 
013104,000235:                                                                                                 #  SGNON          =       VBUF            # TEMP FOR +,- ON
013105,000236:                                                                                                 #  NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
013106,000237:                                                                                                 #  DISTEM =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERB
013107,000238:                                                                                                 #  DECTEM =       VBUF            # COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
013108,000239: 
013109,000240:                                                                                                 #  SGNOFF =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR +,- ON
013110,000241:                                                                                                 #  NVTEMP =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR NVSUB
013111,000242:                                                                                                 #  SFTEMP1        =       VBUF    +1      # STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
013112,000243:                                                                                                 #  HITEMIN        =       VBUF    +1      # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013113,000244:                                                                                                 #                                         #          MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
013114,000245:                                                                                                 #  CODE           =       VBUF    +2      # FOR DSPIN
013115,000246:                                                                                                 #  SFTEMP2        =       VBUF    +2      # STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
013116,000247:                                                                                                 #  LOTEMIN        =       VBUF    +2      # TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013117,000248:                                                                                                 #                                         #          MUST = HITEMIN+1.
013118,000249:                                                                                                 #  MIXTEMP        =       VBUF    +3      # FOR MIXNOUN DATA
013119,000250:                                                                                                 #  SIGNRET        =       VBUF    +3      # RETURN FOR +,- ON
013120,000251: 
013121,000252:                                                                                                 #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
013122,000253: 
013123,000254:                                                                                                 #  ENTRET =       DOTINC          # EXIT FROM ENTER
013124,000255: 
013125,000256:                                                                                                 #  WDCNT          =       DOTRET          # CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
013126,000257:                                                                                                 #  INREL          =       DOTRET          # INPUT BUFFER SELECTION ( X, Y, Z, REG )
013127,000258: 
013128,000259:                                                                                                 #  DSPMMTEM       =       MATINC          # DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
013129,000260:                                                                                                 #  MIXBR          =       MATINC          # INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
013130,000261: 
013131,000262:                                                                                                 #  TEM1           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013132,000263:                                                                                                 #  DSREL          =       TEM1            # REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
013133,000264: 
013134,000265:                                                                                                 #  TEM2           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013135,000266:                                                                                                 #  DSMAG          =       TEM2            # MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
013136,000267:                                                                                                 #  IDADDTEM       =       TEM2            # MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
013137,000268: 
013138,000269:                                                                                                 #  TEM3           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013139,000270:                                                                                                 #  COUNT          =       TEM3            # FOR DSPIN
013140,000271: 
013141,000272:                                                                                                 # # Page 305
013142,000273:                                                                                                 #  TEM4           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013143,000274:                                                                                                 #  LSTPTR =       TEM4            # LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
013144,000275:                                                                                                 #  RELRET =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR RELDSP
013145,000276:                                                                                                 #  FREERET        =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR FREEDSP
013146,000277:                                                                                                 #  DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
013147,000278:                                                                                                 #  SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPSEC
013148,000279:                                                                                                 #  SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            # RETURN FOR SEPMIN
013149,000280: 
013150,000281:                                                                                                 #  TEM5           ERASE                   # EXEC TEMP
013151,000282:                                                                                                 #  NOUNADD        =       TEM5            # TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
013152,000283: 
013153,000284:                                                                                                 #  NNADTEM        ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
013154,000285:                                                                                                 #  NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
013155,000286:                                                                                                 #  IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
013156,000287:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
013157,000288:                                                                                                 #  IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
013158,000289:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
013159,000290:                                                                                                 #  IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR INDIR ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
013160,000291:                                                                                                 #                                         # MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
013161,000292:                                                                                                 #  RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   # TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN ONLY)
013162,000293:                                                                                                 #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013163,000294: 
013164,000295: 
013165,000296:                                                                                                 #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013166,000297: 
013167,000298:                                                                                                 #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013168,000299:                                                                                                 #  BUF, +1, +2
013169,000300:                                                                                                 #  BUF2, +1, +2
013170,000301:                                                                                                 #  MPTEMP
013171,000302:                                                                                                 #  ADDRWD
013172,000303:                                                                                                 #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013173,000304: 
013174,000305: 
013175,000306:                                                                                                 #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013176,000307: 
013177,000308:                                                                                                 #  DSPCNT ERASE                   # COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013178,000309:                                                                                                 #  UPLOCK ERASE                   # BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013179,000310:                                                                                                 #                                         #                                         RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013180,000311:                                                                                                 #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013181,000312: 
013182,000313: 
013183,000314:                                                                                                 #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013184,000315: 
013185,000316:                                                                                                 #  KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013186,000317:                                                                                                 #  DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        # TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013187,000318:                                                                                                 #  KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         # TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013188,000319:                                                                                                 #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013189,000320: 
013190,000321:                                                                                                 # # Page 306
013191,000322:                                                                                                 #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013192,000323:                                                                                                 #  0        10000
013193,000324:                                                                                                 #  1        00001
013194,000325:                                                                                                 #  9        01001
013195,000326:                                                                                                 #  VERB     10001
013196,000327:                                                                                                 #  ERROR RES10010
013197,000328:                                                                                                 #  KEY RLSE 11001
013198,000329:                                                                                                 #  +        11010
013199,000330:                                                                                                 #  -        11011
013200,000331:                                                                                                 #  ENTER    11100
013201,000332:                                                                                                 #  CLEAR    11110
013202,000333:                                                                                                 #  NOUN     11111
013203,000334: 
013204,000335: 
013205,000336:                                                                                                 #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013206,000337:                                                                                                 #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013207,000338:                                                                                                 #  ENERGIZED.
013208,000339:                                                                                                 #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013209,000340:                                                                                                 #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013210,000341:                                                                                                 #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013211,000342: 
013212,000343:                                                                                                 #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013213,000344:                                                                                                 #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
013214,000345:                                                                                                 #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
013215,000346:                                                                                                 #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
013216,000347:                                                                                                 #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
013217,000348:                                                                                                 #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
013218,000349: 
013219,000350:                                                                                                 #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013220,000351:                                                                                                 #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
013221,000352:                                                                                                 #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
013222,000353:                                                                                                 #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
013223,000354:                                                                                                 #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
013224,000355:                                                                                                 #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
013225,000356:                                                                                                 #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
013226,000357:                                                                                                 #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
013227,000358:                                                                                                 #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
013228,000359:                                                                                                 #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
013229,000360:                                                                                                 #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
013230,000361:                                                                                                 #  R1D5  12
013231,000362: 
013232,000363: 
013233,000364:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS AN 11-REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013234,000365: 
013235,000366:                                                                                                 #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
013236,000367:                                                                                                 #  RELADD
013237,000368:                                                                                                 #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
013238,000369:                                                                                                 #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
013239,000370:                                                                                                 #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
013240,000371:                                                                                                 #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)
013241,000372:                                                                                                 # # Page 307
013242,000373:                                                                                                 #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
013243,000374:                                                                                                 #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
013244,000375:                                                                                                 #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
013245,000376:                                                                                                 #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
013246,000377:                                                                                                 #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
013247,000378:                                                                                                 #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
013248,000379:                                                                                                 #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
013249,000380:                                                                                                 #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
013250,000381: 
013251,000382: 
013252,000383:                                                                                                 #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013253,000384:                                                                                                 #  BLANK      00000
013254,000385:                                                                                                 #  0          10101
013255,000386:                                                                                                 #  1          00011
013256,000387:                                                                                                 #  2          11001
013257,000388:                                                                                                 #  3          11011
013258,000389:                                                                                                 #  4          01111
013259,000390:                                                                                                 #  5          11110
013260,000391:                                                                                                 #  6          11100
013261,000392:                                                                                                 #  7          10011
013262,000393:                                                                                                 #  8          11101
013263,000394:                                                                                                 #  9          11111
013264,000395: 
013265,000396: 
013266,000397:                                                                                                 #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013267,000398: 
013268,000399:                                                                                                 #              KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013269,000400:                                                                                                 #              VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013270,000401:                                                                                                 #              OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
013271,000402: 
013272,000403:                                                                                                 # # Page 308
013273,000404: 
013274,000405:                                                                                                 #  START OF EXECUTIVE SECTION OF PINBALL
013275,000406: 
013276,000407: 40,2000                                          BANK     40                                    
013277,000408: 40,2000                                          SETLOC   PINBALL1                              
013278,000409: 40,2000                                          BANK                                           
013279,000410: 
013280,000411: 40,2000                                          COUNT    40/PIN                                
013281,000412: 
013282,000413: 40,2000           34712        CHARIN            CAF      ONE                                   #  BLOCK DISPLAY SYST
013283,000414: 40,2001           57012                          XCH      DSPLOCK                               #  MAKE DSP SYST BUSY, BUT SAVE OLD
013284,000415: 40,2002           54115                          TS       21/22REG                              #  C(DSPLOCK) FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET.
013285,000416: 40,2003           11042                          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ALL KEYS EXCEPT ER TURN ON KR LITE IF
013286,000417: 40,2004           02006                          TC       +2                                    #  CADRSTOR IS FULL.  THIS REMINDS OPERATOR
013287,000418: 40,2005           02013                          TC       CHARIN2                               #  TO RE-ESTABLISH A FLASHING DISPLAY
013288,000419: 40,2006           42057                          CS       ELRCODE1                              #  WHICH HE HAS OBSCURED WITH DISPLAYS OF
013289,000420: 40,2007           60154                          AD       MPAC                                  #  HIS OWN (SEE REMARKS PRECEDING ROUTINE

013346,000477: 
013347,000478: 
013348,000479:                                                                                                 #  NUM ASSEMBLES OCTAL 3 BITS AT A TIME. FOR DECIMAL IT CONVERTS INCOMING
013349,000480:                                                                                                 #  WORD AS A FRACTION, KEEPING RESULTS TO DP.
013350,000481:                                                                                                 #  OCTAL RESULTS ARE LEFT IN XREG, YREG, OR ZREG. HI PART OF DEC IN XREG,
013351,000482:                                                                                                 #  YREG, ZREG. THE LOW PARTS IN XREGLP, YREGLP, OR ZREGLP)
013352,000483:                                                                                                 #  DECBRNCH IS LEFT AT +0 FOR OCT, +1 FOR + DEC, +2 FOR - DEC.
013353,000484:                                                                                                 #  IF DSPCOUNT WAS LEFT -, NO MORE DATA IS ACCEPTED.

013977,001108: 
013978,001109:                                                                                                 # # Page 323
013979,001110:                                                                                                 #            NOUN   TABLES
013980,001111: 
013981,001112:                                                                                                 #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
013982,001113:                                                                                                 #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
013983,001114:                                                                                                 #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
013984,001115:                                                                                                 #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
013985,001116:                                                                                                 #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
013986,001117: 
013987,001118:                                                                                                 #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
013988,001119:                                                                                                 #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
013989,001120: 
013990,001121:                                                                                                 #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
013991,001122: 
013992,001123:                                                                                                 #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
013993,001124:                                                                                                 #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
013994,001125:                                                                                                 #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
013995,001126: 
013996,001127:                                                                                                 #  MIXED-CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
013997,001128:                                                                                                 #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
013998,001129:                                                                                                 #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013999,001130:                                                                                                 #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
014000,001131:                                                                                                 #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014001,001132:                                                                                                 #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
014002,001133: 
014003,001134:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014004,001135:                                                                                                 #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014005,001136:                                                                                                 #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014006,001137:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABEL FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014007,001138:                                                                                                 #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014008,001139: 
014009,001140:                                                                                                 #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
014010,001141:                                                                                                 #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
014011,001142:                                                                                                 #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014012,001143:                                                                                                 #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
014013,001144:                                                                                                 #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014014,001145:                                                                                                 #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014015,001146:                                                                                                 #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
014016,001147:                                                                                                 #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014017,001148: 
014018,001149: 
014019,001150:                                                                                                 #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014020,001151:                                                                                                 #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMONENTS IN NOUN.
014021,001152:                                                                                                 #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014022,001153: 
014023,001154: 
014024,001155:                                                                                                 #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014025,001156:                                                                                                 #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014026,001157: 
014027,001158:                                                                                                 #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014028,001159:                                                                                                 #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
014029,001160: 
014030,001161:                                                                                                 # # Page 324
014031,001162: 
014032,001163:                                                                                                 #            DISPLAY VERBS

015157,002288: 
015158,002289: 
015159,002290:                                                                                                 # # Page 347
015160,002291:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015161,002292:                                                                                                 #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015162,002293:                                                                                                 #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015163,002294:                                                                                                 #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015164,002295:                                                                                                 #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015165,002296: 
015166,002297:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015167,002298:                                                                                                 #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015168,002299:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
015169,002300:                                                                                                 #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
015170,002301:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015171,002302:                                                                                                 #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015172,002303:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILONON.
015173,002304: 
015174,002305:                                                                                                 #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015175,002306:                                                                                                 #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015176,002307:                                                                                                 #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015177,002308: 
015178,002309:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015179,002310:                                                                                                 #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015180,002311: 
015181,002312:                                                                                                 #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015182,002313:                                                                                                 #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
015183,002314: 
015184,002315:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

015314,002445:                                                                                                 #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015315,002446:                                                                                                 #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
015316,002447:                                                                                                 #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
015317,002448: 
015318,002449:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015319,002450: 
015320,002451:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015321,002452:                                                                                                 #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015322,002453:                                                                                                 #            V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015323,002454: 
015324,002455:                                                                                                 #  SUMMARY
015325,002456:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
015326,002457:                                                                                                 #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
015327,002458:

015329,002460: 41,3344           54777                          TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015330,002461: 41,3345           31047                          CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015331,002462: 41,3346           54001                          TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015332,002463: 41,3347           31017                          CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015333,002464: 41,3350           04610                          TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.

015767,002898:
