015769,002900:                                                                                                 #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
015770,002901:                                                                                                 #  END OF LOAD.
015771,002902: 
015772,002903:                                                                                                 # # Page 360
015773,002904:                                                                                                 #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015774,002905: 
015775,002906:                                                                                                 #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015776,002907: 
015777,002908:                                                                                                 #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015778,002909:                                                                                                 #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015779,002910:                                                                                                 #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015780,002911:                                                                                                 #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015781,002912: 
015782,002913:                                                                                                 #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015783,002914:                                                                                                 #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015784,002915:                                                                                                 #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015785,002916: 
015786,002917:                                                                                                 #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015787,002918:                                                                                                 #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015788,002919:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015789,002920:                                                                                                 #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015790,002921:                                                                                                 #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015791,002922:                                                                                                 #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015792,002923:                                                                                                 #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
015793,002924:                                                                                                 #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEOFRE HE OBSCURED
015794,002925:                                                                                                 #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015795,002926:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015796,002927:                                                                                                 #  SUBROUTINES.
015797,002928: 
015798,002929: 40,3362           44710        VBRELDSP          CS       BIT3                                  
015799,002930: 40,3363           00006                          EXTEND                                         
015800,002931: 40,3364           03011                          WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OF UPACT LITE
015801,002932: 40,3365           10115                          CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015802,002933: 40,3366           34675                          CAF      BIT14                                 
015803,002934: 40,3367           71021                          MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015804,002935: 40,3370           10000                          CCS      A                                     
015805,002936: 40,3371           03400                          TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND,
015806,002937: 40,3372           04473        TSTLTS4           TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015807,002938: 40,3373           11042                          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015808,002939: 40,3374           03376                          TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015809,002940: 40,3375           05112                          TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015810,002941: 40,3376           04574                          TC       POSTJUMP                              
015811,002942: 40,3377           21176                          CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015812,002943: 40,3400           34714        UNSUSPEN          CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015813,002944: 40,3401           55012                          TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015814,002945: 40,3402           11042                          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015815,002946: 40,3403           05112                          TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015816,002947: 40,3404           04516                          TC       RELDSP1                               
015817,002948: 40,3405           05112                          TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015818,002949: 
015819,002950: 40,3406                        ENDRELDS          EQUALS                                         
015820,002951: 
015821,002952:                                                                                                 # # Page 361
015822,002953:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
015823,002954:                                                                                                 #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015824,002955:                                                                                                 #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015825,002956:                                                                                                 #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015826,002957:                                                                                                 #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015827,002958: 
015828,002959:                                                                                                 #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WTIH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015829,002960:                                                                                                 #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015830,002961:                                                                                                 #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015831,002962: 
015832,002963:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WTIH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015833,002964:                                                                                                 #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015834,002965: 
015835,002966:                                                                                                 #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015836,002967:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM IS AVAIALBLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015837,002968:                                                                                                 #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015838,002969:                                                                                                 #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
015839,002970:                                                                                                 #  FURTHER ACTION).
015840,002971: 
015841,002972:                                                                                                 #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015842,002973:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015843,002974:                                                                                                 #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015844,002975:                                                                                                 #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015845,002976: 
015846,002977:                                                                                                 #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015847,002978:                                                                                                 #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015848,002979:                                                                                                 #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015849,002980:                                                                                                 #  PROCED WITOHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015850,002981:                                                                                                 #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015851,002982:                                                                                                 #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015852,002983:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR SET UP.
015853,002984: 
015854,002985:                                                                                                 #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015855,002986:                                                                                                 #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015856,002987: 
015857,002988:                                                                                                 #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015858,002989:                                                                                                 #  MONITOR.
015859,002990: 
015860,002991:                                                                                                 #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015861,002992:                                                                                                 #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015862,002993: 
015863,002994:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015864,002995:                                                                                                 #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015865,002996:                                                                                                 #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015866,002997:                                                                                                 #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015867,002998:                                                                                                 #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WTIH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015868,002999:                                                                                                 #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015869,003000:                                                                                                 #  LIGHTS.
015870,003001: 
015871,003002:                                                                                                 #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
015872,003003:                                                                                                 # # Page 362
015873,003004:                                                                                                 #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015874,003005:                                                                                                 #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015875,003006:                                                                                                 #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015876,003007:                                                                                                 #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015877,003008:                                                                                                 #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
015878,003009:                                                                                                 #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015879,003010:                                                                                                 #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015880,003011:                                                                                                 #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015881,003012:                                                                                                 #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015882,003013: 
015883,003014:                                                                                                 #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015884,003015:                                                                                                 #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)

016001,003132:    4220           34674        KILMONON          CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.

016003,003134:                                                                                                 #                                            MONITOR BIT.
016004,003135:    4222           00002                          TC       Q                                     
016005,003136: 
016006,003137: 
016007,003138:                                                                                                 #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
016008,003139:                                                                                                 #             +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016009,003140:                                                                                                 #            -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016010,003141:                                                                                                 #            -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016011,003142:                                                                                                 #               OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
016012,003143: 
016013,003144: 
016014,003145:                                                                                                 #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
016015,003146:                                                                                                 #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016016,003147:                                                                                                 #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016017,003148:                                                                                                 #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016018,003149:                                                                                                 #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016019,003150:                                                                                                 #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016020,003151:                                                                                                 #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
016021,003152:                                                                                                 #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016022,003153:                                                                                                 #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016023,003154:                                                                                                 #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
016024,003155: 
016025,003156:                                                                                                 # # Page 365
016026,003157: 
016027,003158:                                                                                                 #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016028,003159:                                                                                                 #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016029,003160:                                                                                                 #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016030,003161:                                                                                                 #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDDLE.)
016031,003162:                                                                                                 #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016032,003163:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY.
016033,003164: 
016034,003165:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE           LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016035,003166:    4224           04234                          TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016036,003167:    4225           04240                          TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016037,003168:    4226           30001                          CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016038,003169:    4227           74747                          MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016039,003170:    4230           60004                          AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016040,003171:    4231           55042                          TS       CADRSTOR                              
016041,003172:    4232           05070                          TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016042,003173: 
016043,003174: 
016044,003175:    4233           05112        ENDINST           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
016045,003176: 
016046,003177: 
016047,003178:    4234           11042        ISCADR+0          CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016048,003179:    4235           04243                          TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

016390,003521: 
016391,003522:                                                                                                 # # Page 373
016392,003523:                                                                                                 #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016393,003524: 
016394,003525:                                                                                                 #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016395,003526:                                                                                                 #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016396,003527:                                                                                                 #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016397,003528:                                                                                                 #  OFFERED.
016398,003529: 
016399,003530:                                                                                                 #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY TEH KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016400,003531:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
016401,003532:                                                                                                 #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
016402,003533:                                                                                                 #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016403,003534:                                                                                                 #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016404,003535:                                                                                                 #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016405,003536:                                                                                                 #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016406,003537: 
016407,003538: 
016408,003539:                                                                                                 #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016409,003540:                                                                                                 #            CAF    V/N
016410,003541:                                                                                                 #  L         TC     NVSUB
016411,003542:                                                                                                 #  L+1       RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016412,003543:                                                                                                 #  L+2       RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016413,003544: 
016414,003545: 
016415,003546:                                                                                                 #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
016416,003547:                                                                                                 #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016417,003548:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016418,003549:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016419,003550:                                                                                                 #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016420,003551: 
016421,003552: 
016422,003553:                                                                                                 #          THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016423,003554:                                                                                                 #            CAF    WAKEFCADR
016424,003555:                                                                                                 #            TC     NVSUBUSY
016425,003556: 
016426,003557: 
016427,003558:                                                                                                 #  .
016428,003559: 
016429,003560: 
016430,003561:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016431,003562:                                                                                                 #  IS NOT USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
016432,003563:                                                                                                 #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016433,003564:                                                                                                 #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016434,003565: 
016435,003566: 
016436,003567:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016437,003568:                                                                                                 #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MAKE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016438,003569:                                                                                                 #  WHEN
016439,003570:                                                                                                 #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016440,003571:                                                                                                 #     IS EXCEEDED.
016441,003572:                                                                                                 #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
016442,003573:                                                                                                 # # Page 374
016443,003574:                                                                                                 #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016444,003575: 
016445,003576:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY          CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016446,003577:    4454           60002                          AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
016447,003578:    4455           60004                          AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016448,003579:    4456           04574        NVSUBUSY          TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016449,003580:    4457           10550                          CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016450,003581:    4460           02003        2K+3              OCT      2003                                  
016451,003582: 
016452,003583:                                                                                                 #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016453,003584:                                                                                                 #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016454,003585: 
016455,003586: 04,2550                                          SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016456,003587: 04,2550                                          COUNT    07/PIN                                
016457,003588: 
016458,003589: 04,2550           54001        NVSUBSY1          TS       L                                     
016459,003590: 04,2551           04234                          TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016460,003591: 04,2552           04240                          TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016461,003592: 04,2553           04410                          TC       RELDSPON                              
016462,003593: 04,2554           30001                          CA       L                                     
016463,003594: 04,2555           55043                          TS       DSPLIST                               
016464,003595: 04,2556           05070        ENDNVBSY          TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016465,003596: 
016466,003597: 
016467,003598:                                                                                                 #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016468,003599:                                                                                                 #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016469,003600:                                                                                                 #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016470,003601:                                                                                                 #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016471,003602:                                                                                                 #  IS NOT BUSY.
016472,003603: 
016473,003604:    4461                                          SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016474,003605:    4461                                          COUNT    02/PIN                                
016475,003606: 
016476,003607:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT          LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016477,003608:    4462           54123                          TS       NVTEMP                                
016478,003609:    4463           34675                          CAF      BIT14                                 
016479,003610:    4464           71021                          MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016480,003611:    4465           61012                          AD       DSPLOCK                               
016481,003612:    4466           10000                          CCS      A                                     
016482,003613:    4467           14471                          TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016483,003614:    4470           14200                          TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016484,003615:                                                                                                 #                                           AFTER EXECUTION.
016485,003616:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1           INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016486,003617:    4472           14453                          TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016487,003618: 
016488,003619: 
016489,003620:                                                                                                 #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016490,003621:                                                                                                 #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016491,003622:                                                                                                 #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016492,003623:    4473           56002        RELDSP            XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
016493,003624:                                                                                                 # # Page 375
016494,003625:    4474           54144                          TS       RELRET                                #  OFF,  SEARCH DSPLIST
016495,003626:    4475           44675                          CS       BIT14                                 
016496,003627:    4476           00004                          INHINT                                         
016497,003628:    4477           71021                          MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016498,003629:    4500           55021                          TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016499,003630:    4501           11043                          CCS      DSPLIST                               
016500,003631:    4502           04504                          TC       +2                                    
016501,003632:    4503           04507                          TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016502,003633:    4504           34714                          CAF      ZERO                                  
016503,003634:    4505           57043                          XCH      DSPLIST
